</div> </div> </div> <div class="CategoryFooterDescription"><span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxCategory_lblCategoryCustom1"><h3><font style="color: #ff0000;">ALL NFA RULES APPLY</font>- PLEASE READ THE <a href="http://impactguns.com/content.aspx?page=howtoorder#class3" target="_blank">CLASS 3 ORDERING PROCEDURES</a></h3> <p>An A.O.W. is a weapon classification utilized by the B.A.T.F. to categorize and restrict those weapons that are not considered to be a rifle, pistol, or machinegun. An example of an A.O.W. is a short-barreled shotgun or a pen-gun. They are class III (NFA) items, and must be approved for transfer to individuals at the federal level (with a "form-4"). Cost to transfer= $5.00<br> <strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><strong>S.B.S. - Short Barrel Shotgun</strong><br> Short barrel shotguns will have a barrel less than 18", and will have a full stock. These guns require a $200.00 transfer tax.</p></span></div> </div> </div> </div> <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript"> var theForm = document.forms[0]; if(theForm != null) theForm.action = "";
